So all-aboard one of our cruises for a seat to one of the greatest shows on earth. You have to sail it to believe it.

          document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', function(){

             mobileFirst   : true,

             arrows        : true,
             dots          : false,
             adaptiveHeight: true,
             slidesToShow: 3,
             infinite: false,
             responsive: [
                 {
                     breakpoint: 769,
                     settings: {
                         slidesToShow: 2,
                         slidesToScroll: 1,

                         arrows: false,
                         dots: true
                     }
                 },

                     breakpoint: 500,
                     settings: {
                         slidesToShow: 1,
                         slidesToScroll: 1,
                         infinite: false,
                         arrows: true,
                         dots: true
                     }
                 }]
         } );
         if (jQuery(window).width() >= 1230) {
             jacobiteInterface.parallaxScroll('.js-parallax');
         }
         jQuery('#search').submit(function(e){
             if ((jQuery('#adults').val() == 0) && (jQuery('#senior').val() == 0) && (jQuery('#students').val() == 0)) {
                 alert('Please choose at least one passenger of adult age.');
                 return false;
             }
         });
         jacobiteInterface.noTouchClass();
         jQuery('#manage-booking').submit(function(e){
             e.preventDefault();
             location.href = 'https://secure.jacobite.co.uk/MyBooking/Home/findbooking?email='+jQuery('#manage-booking #email').val()+'&reservationID='+jQuery('#manage-booking #reservation-number').val();
         });
 
         if ($(window).width() >= 768) {
             jQuery( '.mh-signposts' ).matchHeight();
         }
